 philhal police ab is baat kii taftish kar rahi he ki kya todphod main kuch or log bhi shaamil the or agar haa to jald se jald un logon ko bhi salaakhon ke peeche pahunchaaya ja sake
 Two days later, on September 28, it is the birthday of Bollywood handsome hunk Ranbir Kapoor
 bollywood kii nai peedi ke actors main ranbir kaaphi popular hai, lekin kapur khandaan ke liye unki ahmiyat isse kahin zyada he
 Why not? He is the eyeglass of the Kapoor family
 haalanki karishma or karina ne bhi kapur khandaan kii filmi viraasat ko aage le jane kaa kaam bakhubi kiya he, magar dada raaj kapur kaa sabase zyada lagaav ranbir se tha
 It is said that when Ranbir was born, there was no place for Raj Kapoor's happiness
 iskaa zikr ranbir ke papa rishi kapur kii autobiography 'khullam khulla' main bhi miltaa he
 Ranbir was eagerly waiting for Ranbir in 1982
 unase pehle unki bahan riddhimaa 1980 main paidaa hui thim
 But it is said that the atmosphere of happiness in the family was different at the time of Ranbir's birth
 isaki khaas vajah bhi thi
 Before Ranbir, he had no grandson to call Raj Kapoor as his grandfather
 rishi kapur kii bahan ke bacchon ke saath sarnem kapur nahin judaa tha
 Then Dhabbu ji i
e
 Randhir Kapoor's two daughters Karishma and Kareena's surname were also going to change after marriage
 aise main shaayad raaj kapur ko apane family tree ke liye ek pote kaa besabri se intjaar tha
 The wait ended on the birth of Ranbir
 ranbir kapur ne 'i dil he mushkil' ke set par manaaya berth derishi ne apni kitaab khullam-khulla main raaj kapur ke ranbir se is pyaar ke bare main kai baaten bataai hai
 One of them is related to his will
 vaise to ranbir ke paas kapur khandaan kii vajah se cinema kii ek aseem viraasat he
 But apart from this, Raj Kapoor in his will wrote many valuable gifts to Ranbir
 viraasat main mili anmol tohfeinamein se ek he kapur khandaan kaa khandaani sone kaa sikaa
 There are some letters in Afghani on it
 bataa den ki kapur parivaar kaa sambandh peshawar se he
 Ranbir Kapoor's great-grandfather Basaveshwar Nath Kapoor was the tehsildar in Peshawar
 peshawar north west frontier provinance main sthit he
 Its border is with Afghanistan
 bataaya jaataa he ki sone ke us sikke ke alaava sone ke sikkon kaa ek necoles bhi raaj kapur ne ranbir ko hi diya tha
 Pictures of Kareena Kapoor's birthday celebrations came out, it is clear that this legacy will be carried forward from generation to generation, but the feeling that Ranbir Kapoor got will remain only on his part and will remain priceless
 portugal ke purv pradhanmantri antonio guteres ko guuruuvaar ko mahasabha ne sanyukt raashtra kaa aglaa mahasachiv niyukt kiya
 The powerful General Assembly, consisting of 193 member countries, accepted the proposal to appoint 67-year-old Guterres as the ninth United Nations secretary-general
 vah baan kii moon kii jagah lenge jinka kaarykaal 31 disambar ko puraa hoga
 The 15-member UN Security Council voted for Guterres last week and sent his name to the General Assembly
 guteres 1995 se lekar 2002 tak portugal ke pradhanmantri the
 He was also the United Nations High Commissioner for Refugee Affairs from June 2005 to December 2015
 mahasachiv kaa chayan karne ke liye parishad main hue sabhi chah anaupchaarik matadaanon main guteres sabase aage rahe
 He was ahead at a time when many member countries and civil society organizations of the United Nations were raising demands to elect a woman as the head of the world body
 sanyukt raashtra ke 71 saal ke itihaas main iske sabhi pramukh purush hi rahe hai
 Ban, however, called him "a great choice" for the post of general secretary
 baan ne sanyukt raashtra sharnaarthi agency ke pramukh ke rup main guteres ke kaarykaal kaa sandarbh dete hue kaha, ''mahasachiv-nirvaachit guteres ko ham sabhi acchhee tarah jaanate hai
 But he is perhaps best known where it matters most (on the fronts of armed struggle and human suffering)
 '' He said last week that Guterres showed "deep compassion for the millions who have been forced to leave their homes
" unhone unki madad ke liye anwarat kaam kiya
 "his (guterres's) previous experience as Prime Minister of Portugal, his extensive knowledge of world affairs and his lively intelligence as well as his ability to lead the United Nations at a very important time," Ban had said
 Will help '' Speaking in Lisbon shortly after his selection last week, Guterres expressed "gratitude" and resolved to "serve" for the most vulnerable sections, including victims of conflict, terrorism, human rights violations and poverty
 april main rakhe gaye apane drushti patr main unhone jor dekar kaha tha ki charter main nihit shanti, nyaay, maanviya garima, sahansheeltaa or ekajutata ke mulya vishwa main sabhi samskritiyon or dharmon kaa centre hai tathaa inaki jhalak ''upanishdon se lekar quran tathaa gaspal tak main dikhti he
 "guterres said that the UN secretary-general should" actively, relentlessly and tirelessly "do his good work and mediation ability like an honest arbitrator
 unhone yah bhi kaha tha ki aatankwaad se ladane ke liye rokthaam bhi mahatvapurn he tathaa antarrashtriya samudaay ko sabhi tarah ke aatankwaad ko ukhaad phenkane ke liye samuhik rup se kaam karne kaa ''kanoonee adhikaar he'' or yah uskaa ''naitik daayitv'' he
 As part of the procedures to appoint a new head of the world body, a draft proposal is issued to take action for the General Assembly, after a recommendation is sent from the Council to the General Assembly
 pichley paanch mahasachiv mahasabha ne aam sahmati se sweekaar kiye ek prastaav ke jariye niyukt kiye the 
 Voting is conducted only when a member country demands it and the General Assembly will need a simple majority to accept the motion
 yadi matdaan karaayaa jaataa he to yah gupt matdaan hoga
 Apart from Guterres, 12 other candidates were also in the race for the post
 nae sanyukt raashtra mahasachiv ke chayan kaa faisla paaramparik rup se kuch shaktishaalee desh band kamaron main hui baithkon main karte the, lekin is baar pehali baar is prakriya main jan charchaa shaamil hui or prayek ummidavaar ne vishwa ke shirshatam rajanyik pad ke liye prachaar kiya 
 Russian diplomats at the United Nations and the Council for the month of October told reporters last week that Guterres has "many strong qualifications" to lead the United Nations
 ummidavaaron, sanyukt raashtra ke sadsy deshon or naagarik samaaj ke sanghathanon ke bich anaupchaarik charchaa april main shuru hui thi jab pehle teen ummidavaaron ne apana drushti patr rakhaa tathaa is mudde par sawaalon ke jawaab die ki ve kis tarah satat vikaas ko badhaava denge, kis tarah shanti prayaason main sudhaar karenge, kis tarah maanavadhikaron kii raksha karenge or kis tarah maanviya aapadaaon se niptenge 
 The comments iske atirikt july main sanyukt raashtra ne mahasabha haul main pehali baar apni tarah kii charchaa karai jiskaa prasaaran vishvabhar main televijan par kiya gaya or iskaa web prasaaran bhi kiya gaya
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) 15 sadasyeey sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad ne pichley saptaah guteres ke liye matdaan kiya tha or unka naam mahasabha ko bhej diya tha
 Guterres was Prime Minister of Portugal from 1995 to 2002
 vah june 2005 se disambar 2015 tak sharnaarthi maamalon ke sanyukt raashtra ucchayukta bhi rahe
 Guterres was at the forefront of all six informal elections in the council to elect the secretary-general
 vah aise samay aage rahe jab sanyukt raashtra ke kai sadsy desh or naagarik samaaj sanghathan vishwa nikaay kaa mukhiya kisi mahila ko chunane kii maang uthaa rahe the
 In the 71-year history of the United Nations, all its leading men have been
 haalanki, baan ne unhen mahasachiv pad ke liye ''ek shandaar vikalp'' qaraar diya
 Referring to Guterres' tenure as head of the United Nations Refugee Agency, Ban said, "we all know the secretary-general-elected Guterres very well
" lekin vah shaayad sarvshereshth rup main vahaan jane jate hai jahaan iskaa sarvaadhik mahatv ho (sashastr sangharsh or maanviya pidaa ke morchon par) 
 '' unhone pichley saptaah kaha tha ki guteres ne ''lakhon logon ke liye gahari karunaa dikhaai jinhen apane ghar chhodane ko majaboor hona padaa he
 He worked relentlessly to help her
 '' baan ne kaha tha, ''portugal ke pradhanmantri ke rup main unka (guteres kaa) pichhlaa anubhav, vishwa maamalon ke bare main unka vyapak gyaan or unki jeevant medha ek atyant mahatvapurn samay main sanyukt raashtra kaa netritv karne main bhi unki acchhee tarah madad karegi
 '' pichley saptaah apane chayan ke turant baad lisbon main bolte hue guteres ''aabhaar'' prakat kiya tha or sangharsh, aatankwaad, maanavadhikaar ulanghan tathaa garibi ke pedishon sahit atyant samvedansheel tabakon ke liye ''seva karne'' kaa sankalp liya tha
 In his vision letter in April, he stressed that the values of peace, justice, human dignity, tolerance and solidarity enshrined in the Charter are the center of all cultures and religions in the world, and their glimpse "from the Upanishads to the Quran and the Gospel" i see
 '' guteres ne kaha tha ki sanyukt raashtra mahasachiv ko apane achche kaaryon tathaa madhyasthata kshamta ko ek eemaandaar madhyasth kii tarah ''sakriyata, nirantarata or bina thake'' karnaa chahie
 He also said that prevention is also important to fight terrorism and that the international community has a "legal right" to work collectively to eliminate all forms of terrorism, and that it has a "moral obligation"
 is
 vishwa nikaay kaa nayaa pramukh niyukt karne kii prakriyaaon ke tahat, parishad se mahasabha ko sifarish bheje jane ke baad, mahasabha ke liye karrwai karne ke vaaste ek masauda prastaav jari kiya jaataa he
 The last five general secretaries were appointed by the General Assembly through a resolution accepted by consensus
 matdaan tabhi karaayaa jaataa he jab koi sadsy desh isaki maang kare or prastaav ko sweekaar karne ke liye mahasabha ko ek saadhaaran bahumat kii aavashyaktaa hogi
 If voted on, it will be a secret ballot
 guteres ke atirikt 12 anya ummidavaar bhi pad kii daud main the
 The selection of the new United Nations secretary-general was traditionally decided by some powerful countries in closed-door meetings, but this time for the first time the process involved public discussion and each candidate campaigned for the world's top-most diplomatic post
 sanyukt raashtra main roosi rajanyik evam oktober maheene ke liye parishad ne pichley saptaah samvaadadaataaon se kaha tha ki sanyukt raashtra kaa netritv karne ke liye guteres main ''kai majboot yogyataayen'' hai 
 Informal discussions between the candidates, UN member states and civil society organizations began in April when the first three candidates placed their vision papers and answered questions on the issue of how they would promote sustainable development
 Will improve peace efforts, how to protect human rights and how to deal with human disasters
 tippaniyan In addition, in July, the United Nations held its first-of-its-kind discussion in the General Assembly Hall, which was broadcast worldwide on television and also broadcast on the web

 The selection of the new United Nations secretary-general was traditionally decided by some powerful countries in closed-door meetings, but this time for the first time the process involved public discussion and each candidate campaigned for the world's top-most diplomatic post

 bihar ke party maamalon ke prabharee shaktisingh gohil ne shanivaar ko bataaya ki gathbandhan ke saajhedaaron jaise tejasvi yadav, upendra kushvaha or jeethanram maanjhi ko is kaarykram ke liye nimantran bheja gaya he
 The Congress is part of the Grand Alliance of Bihar
 is mahagathbandhan main rajd, ralospa, echeem bhi hai

 dekhne kii baat yah he ki police karrwai main ghayal hue kushvaha kaarykram main ja paayenge yaa nahin
 However, no official statement has come about RJD leader Tejashwi Yadav taking part in the event

 The Congress has named this rally as 'jan Akanksha Rally'
 is raily ko ko lekar jahaan congress ke netaa or kaaryakarta utsahit hai, vahiin isamen bhaag lene ke liye log ek din pehle hi patna pahunchane lage hai

 He held discussions with collectors, applicants, operators and concerned staff at public service centers in Gwalior, Shivpuri, Hoshangabad, Jabalpur, Indore and Jhabua
 lok seva diwas par pehle din aparaahn paanch baje tak 55 lok seva kendron kaa sanchaalan shuru ho gaya

 He said that if people could get services without any hassle on time, then it would be a revolutionary step to put the concept of Ram Rajya into practice

 ' rojio ne kaha ki yah keval kashmir yaa pakistan kaa maamla nahin he
 Kashmiri terrorist organizations, which have received assistance from the Government of Pakistan, have their base in Afghanistan
 unhone kaha, 'main samoohon kii suchi bana saktaa hum
 lashkar-e-taiba, Harkat ul Mujahideen, whom the Ministry of External Affairs said in 2014 that they are running training camps in Afghanistan
 ye samooh america javaanon par hamalaa kar rahe hai or unki hatya kar rahe he
 i have not even talked about organizations like Taliban, Haqqani network or Mulla Nazir group
 ye keval chote samooh hai
 ' rojio ne aarope lagaaya ki pakistan shandaar tareeke se ek chhadam khel khel rahaa he

 acha taliban har vah samooh he jise pakistan pasand karata he or jo samooh pakistan par hamalaa nahin karata

 hakkaani network, afgaan taliban, mullah nazeer samooh

 ' He said, 'pakistan did not mention the name of any major, middle level or lower level leader killed in these campaigns because he did not kill anyone
 unhone kisi ko giraftaar nahin kiya

 ' rojio ne kaha ki ve in samoohon kaa samarthan isliye karte hai kyonki unhen lagata he ki bharat kaa saamana karne ke liye unke paas yah sabase acha avasar he
